British Army Budget Totals £49 Million 55

London: The 1936 army budget totals £49,201,000, an increase of £5,730,000 over last year. Of this, £1,555,000 is the cost of special projects adopted due to the Italo-Ethiopian dispute. This budget does not include the cost of expanding national defense as proposed in the government's white paper. Secretary of State for War Cooper said in his statement that it has been decided to establish a mechanized automatic team supplemented by a tank brigade in the existing cavalry division, and it has been decided to convert the infantry into three brigades, each with three rifle battalions and one machine gun battalion. The number of army personnel will increase by 6,200 to 158,000 to provide for air defense development, naval defense renovation, overseas fortified port garrisons, and the allocation needed during army conscription. More powerful anti-aircraft guns are being tested. The army's air defense equipment is being implemented. The general allocation of major infantry battalions is largely the same as in 1935, except that an infantry battalion will be stationed in Malaya. Due to the situation overseas, the army has already made temporary allocations. Light artillery brigades will be converted into field artillery brigades, equipped with four-point-five howitzers and one eighteen-pound heavy gun. The manufacturing of new Bran-type machine guns is currently in preparation. Anti-tank rifles have now been adopted as the first line of defense against armored vehicles. The latest light tanks, which have proven effective, will continue to be manufactured this year. Other new tanks and armored vehicles will also be tested soon. New machine gun mounts have been tested and have achieved excellent results. Small four-wheeled vehicles used for the first line of transport have now been developed to the point where they can replace horses. A type of wheeled vehicle has been tested in the cavalry and has performed very well in the fields. This year, it is planned to use it in a regiment to tow field guns. A six-wheeled light vehicle is also being tested. At the beginning of this year, the regular army will be 10,000 men short of its authorized strength, and 26,000 men will be discharged during the year, so 36,000 new recruits will be needed. There has been a severe shortage of volunteers in recent years, but the physical fitness of new recruits is now improving. The army reserve can be increased to 8,000 men. (Reuters, 5th)

Anglo-German Naval Agreement; Negotiations Underway; All Points Agreed by the Three Nations; Germany Did Not Raise Objections; Russia Informed of Progress 57

London: This afternoon, German Ambassador to the UK, Herr von Hoesch, accompanied by Naval Attaché Wiesner of the Embassy, held talks at the Admiralty with First Lord of the Admiralty, Lord Monsell, Chief of Naval Staff, Admiral Chatfield, and naval expert from the Foreign Office, Craige. The British representatives informed Ambassador Hoesch of the results of the recent discussions between the delegations of the UK, France, and the United States. It is reported that Germany did not raise any substantial objections to any of the points already agreed upon by the UK, France, and the United States. However, it expressed hesitation about the UK and Germany signing a bilateral agreement before the Soviet Union agrees to conclude a similar agreement. As for the issue of quantitative limitations, Germany has not raised it at this time, nor has it insisted that the Soviet Union must accept quantitative limitations, which is contrary to initial expectations. In the UK, it is believed that future naval treaties contain safeguard clauses, and if any clause in the naval treaty is not complied with by any country, Germany and other signatory countries will demand revisions based on the safeguard clauses. Therefore, the issue of the Soviet Union accepting quantitative limitations does not need to be raised. (It means that if the Soviet Navy expands significantly in the future, Germany can demand revisions to the naval treaty.) So far, the UK has not formally consulted with the Soviet Union on the issue of concluding a bilateral agreement between the UK and Russia, but is only informing the Soviet Union of the progress of the naval negotiations at any time. (Havas, 4th)

London: Foreign Under-Secretary of State, Lord Stanhope, met with Mr Corbin, the chief French representative at the Naval Conference, this afternoon to inform him of the exchange of views between the UK and Germany, and to inform him that the UK is now planning to contact the Soviet Union on the issue of concluding a bilateral naval agreement between the UK and Russia. Naval circles here are quite optimistic about the signing of the future naval treaty, believing that if no unexpected complications arise, all major technical difficulties have been resolved. The so-called unexpected complications are that Germany may raise new demands for signing an Anglo-German agreement, but there is no indication of this at this time. The U.S. delegation sent a request to Washington today, and it is now known that the instruction sought is only for the drafting of the naval treaty and is not related to any major issues. (Havas, 4th)

Italy and Albania Sign Agreement to Resolve Disputes; Granting of Timber and Mineral Rights in Exchange for Financial Assistance 59

Paris: Albania, on the eastern coast of the Adriatic Sea, was recognized as an independent state by the Paris Ambassadors' Conference (1921) and was allowed to join the League of Nations as a member. Italy then concluded a military alliance treaty with Albania in 1927 and signed the Treaties of Tirana with Albania in 1926 and 1927, stipulating that Italy would provide Albania with a certain amount of financial assistance annually. However, since 1932, the payments have stopped, leading to disputes between the two countries. According to a report in the Paris Echo, after lengthy negotiations, Italy and Albania signed an agreement yesterday to end the dispute. According to this agreement, the Italian government will still provide Albania with no more than eight million lire annually, and King Zog I of Albania will use this money for the construction of highways and the improvement of the port of Durrës, and will hire Italian technicians to assist in the management. Albania will grant Italy the general rights to forests and mines. It seems that Italy, whose influence in the Balkans has long declined, is allowed to rebuild its power. Since Turkey joined the Balkan Entente last spring, Italy has lost influence, and it wants to revitalize it, and it will have the opportunity to actively act again. (Havas dispatch, 5th)

United States Purchases Newly Mined Silver from Canada; To Achieve a Gold-Silver Ratio of Three to One 60

The U.S. Treasury Department announced today that the purchase of newly mined silver from Canada will now be handled entirely by the Bank of Canada, the same as the method used by the United States in Mexico. This move has no special significance, but is merely intended to concentrate the purchase of new Canadian silver at market prices. According to some observers, the U.S. Treasury Department has an agreement with Canada stipulating that the U.S. Treasury Department will purchase all or part of the silver produced in Canada. Canada's annual silver production is 16,400,000 ounces. Now, all the silver produced in the United States and Mexico is owned by the U.S. Treasury Department. If Canada's production is also purchased by the United States, the U.S. Treasury Department will hold 63% of the world's total silver production. It is widely believed that the new U.S.-Canada agreement must contain a method for the U.S. Treasury Department to gradually withdraw from the world silver market. (Reuters dispatch, 4th)

Washington: It was announced here today that the U.S. government will soon purchase newly produced raw silver from Canada. Treasury Secretary Morgenthau has instructed the Federal Reserve Bank of New York to act as the Treasury Department's agent and purchase from the Bank of Canada, with market prices as the standard. The impact of this move on the U.S. silver purchase policy is still unclear today. Treasury Department officials said that the new plan does not hinder the government from continuing to purchase Canada's existing silver. It is understood that the Treasury Department will proceed on both fronts, purchasing all new and existing silver from around the world, and may still purchase futures in the Montreal market. Non-official sources said that the Treasury Department has not stipulated the amount of Canadian raw silver to be purchased. The Treasury Department claims that this move will not have much impact on the silver purchase policy. (National News Agency dispatch, 4th)

Hebei Province Actively Prevents Communism; Implements Regional Suppression Methods; Rectifies Security Regiments Throughout the Province 67

Tianjin Communication: Since the disturbance caused by Liu Guitang's bandit forces in Hebei Province, it took more than forty days to quell the rebellion, with great effort and expense. However, the defeated bandits fled in all directions, scattered in Qingyuan, Julu, Nanhe, Dacheng, and other places, colluding with local gentry and bandits. Although they do not dare to openly rebel, hidden dangers remain, and they may attempt to cause trouble at any time. However, this is not the most serious problem. What is currently sufficient to plunge Hebei Province into great chaos is the communist bandits in southern and central Hebei. This is because the Sichuan bandits fled north, encroaching on Shanxi and Shaanxi. Their mobile detachments infiltrated Hebei Province, inciting ignorant people to riot, in order to hinder the implementation of the North China anti-communist plan. According to recent investigations by the authorities, communist bandits have a general headquarters in Shunde, and branch offices in Yaoshan, Renqiu, Julu, Renxian, Daming, Qingfeng, and other counties. The pseudo-chief Liu Wenzhong calls himself the commander-in-chief of the pseudo-Red Army, and the pseudo-deputy chief Liu Zhenru calls himself the commander of the guerrillas. A pseudo-guerrilla headquarters has been established in Longping County, gathering more than 2,000 pseudo-soldiers. In addition, scattered bandits such as Liu Guitang and Liu Zhinan, as well as gang bandits such as the Yellow Sand Society, Red Spear Society, and Jinsheng Tao from the Daming area, have been recruited and organized into black teams, lurking near Shunde, under the command of Liu Wenzhong, commander-in-chief of the pseudo-Red Army, to act together. Shunde, Daming, and more than twenty other counties have suffered years of famine and the people are living in misery. Moreover, after being burned and looted by bandits such as Liu Guitang and Liu Zhinan, the situation has become even more dire, with most families impoverished and unable to make a living. Once communist bandits promote and incite riots, it is extremely easy to succeed. Therefore, the people in Xingtai, Baoding, and nearby counties are all in an unstable state. The Hebei Provincial Government is also fully aware of the dangerous situation. Therefore, in addition to dividing the province into four regions and making every effort to search and suppress bandit forces, it has also clarified the responsibilities of the various armies stationed in the province. After the anti-bandit responsibilities within each region have been divided, the provincial authorities are still worried that the arrangements are not thorough enough. At the end of last month, Zhang Yunrong, the provincial security commander, representing Song Zheyuan, chairman of the provincial government, convened a meeting of responsible officers in Baoding. Many resolutions were made regarding the suppression of bandits and the maintenance of public security. The officers of each army division have returned to their defenses to carry out strict deployment. The provincial government is still worried that the precautions are not sufficient, giving the communist bandits an opportunity to take advantage. It has ordered each county to recruit strong men separately and organize them into security regiments, under the direct jurisdiction of the security commander. They are collectively referred to as security regiments, and all command authority is under the command of the security commander Zhang Yunrong. The funding for the militia in each county will also be transferred to the province in the future, and each regiment will directly apply to the security command headquarters for payment, eliminating the need for county governments to impose levies on the people on various pretexts. The provincial authorities believe that Guangxi is the best in the country in organizing militias and intend to send personnel to investigate and learn from it. According to the provincial authorities, before the communist disaster becomes serious, Hebei and Chahar provinces will first strengthen their forces by rectifying national defense. With adequate preparations, they will prevent external communist bandits from crossing the Lei Pool even one step and continue to search and suppress internal communist bandits to prevent them from spreading. At the same time, Daming, Handan, and other counties in southern Hebei, which border Shandong Province, will install long-distance telephones and adopt a policy of close contact. In the event of an incident, communication will be smooth, and responses will be swift. The wiring is being rushed from the Daming side. (3rd)

Matsui Iwane Arrives in Xiamen; Directs Japanese to Establish the Asia Association; Leaves for Fuzhou by Boat After Staying in Xiamen for One Day 68

Xiamen Communication: Japanese Army General Matsui Iwane toured Hebei, Shandong, and other provinces last winter, advocating the Greater Asia Doctrine. On the 2nd of this month, he traveled south from Tokyo, passing through Guangdong and Guangxi. On the morning of the 1st of this month, he took a Shanghai-Guangdong flight from Guangdong and arrived in Xiamen at 10:00 am. Japanese Consul in Xiamen Yamada Yoshitaro, Chairman of the Japanese Residents Association Takemura Masahide, Chairman of the Taiwan Public Association Lin Mutu, as well as Japanese and Taiwanese residents, all went to the seaplane station to welcome him. After Matsui got off the plane, he went to the Japanese Consulate first. At noon, he attended a banquet hosted by the Taiwan Strait Public Association and the Bank of Taiwan at the Seaside Hotel. At 2:00 pm, he convened a meeting of Japanese and Taiwanese people at the Yamato Club on Gulangyu to prepare for the organization of the Xiamen Greater Asia Association. Takemura Masahide was elected chairman, and the following matters were resolved: 1. The chairman shall nominate the drafters of the association rules and the directors. 2. The association shall be an independent group in Xiamen. 3. The association shall be established at the end of this month or the beginning of next month. 4. The membership fee shall be ten yuan per year. 5. Members must be recommended by two officers before they can join. It was decided that Matsui would recount his travels to the south and the Greater Asia Association. He said, "At the end of last year, I toured Manchuria and North China for two months. This time, I will visit Fujian, Guangdong, and Guangxi in South China, meeting with various important people and various sectors of the people. All of them greatly resonated with my advocacy of the Greater Asia Doctrine. China and Japan have had contact for more than 2,000 years, but the relations between the two countries have never been as treacherous as in recent years. I dare not claim that Japan is completely right. Both sides have responsibilities and need to reflect on them. Although there are various reasons, since the Eastern invasion of Europeanization, many people who are obsessed with Europe and the United States have forgotten the ancient Eastern morals and culture. It is also possible that the actions and ideas and political relations between governments have caused such estrangement. Fujian and Taiwan are not only geographically close, but also have many ethnic ties. They are truly inseparable. My advocacy of the Greater Asia Doctrine over the years is based on this viewpoint. Xiamen is the economic center of Fujian and has an important relationship with Taiwan. I hope you will work hard." Then, Taketoh, a member of the Asia Association who traveled with Matsui, gave a speech, congratulating the recent establishment of the Xiamen Greater Asia Association. It was found that the Xiamen Greater Asia Association was established because Matsui, when he previously passed through Xiamen on his way to Guangdong, instructed the Japanese and Taiwanese people in Xiamen to organize it in advance. A preparatory committee was immediately established. Now that Matsui has come again, he has concluded the preparatory work and scheduled the establishment. During Matsui's stay in Xiamen, he did not socialize with people from all walks of life. On the 2nd, Matsui took the Haiyang ship to the province. (5th)

Anhai, Quanzhou; Smugglers Operate Private Companies; Large-Scale, Closely Organized; Smugglers Collude with Local Residents and Share Profits 69

Xiamen Communication: In Xiamen and along the coasts of southern Fujian, Zhangzhou, and Quanzhou, the practice of tax evasion and smuggling has been extremely prevalent in recent years. Although customs patrol ships have been cracking down severely and making continuous seizures, it has not been curbed much. At the end of last month, the Third Pacification Command of Quanzhou cracked down on a large-scale smuggling organization, Nanshun Trading Company, in Shishi, which was one of them. Recently, it has been further discovered that there is an even larger-scale smuggling company in Tatu Township, Anhai, outside the South Gate of Quanzhou. The organization and content of the company were found to have been established in Shanyao, Huian County three years ago. In July of last year, it was moved to Yongning Port, Jinjiang. In January of this year, it was moved to Tatu Township, Anhai. Recently, a certain seafood shop owner from Kaiyuan Road, Xiamen, and a national from a certain country invested heavily to expand the organization and connect with smugglers from various places. Four small smuggling companies were merged into this large-scale organization. One of the four small companies is on Kaiyuan Road in Xiamen, one was founded by a national from a certain country, one is operated by smugglers from Daku, Huian County, and one is a powerful smuggler in Tatu, Anhai. The capital is 600,000 yuan, of which 300,000 yuan has already been collected. The remaining shares are reserved for influential parties to join. A week ago, several smugglers from Xiamen, along with a dozen or so nationals from a certain country, went to Quanzhou and stayed for several days. Their mission was to solicit shares for the company. The company uses sailboats exclusively for smuggling. It owns more than 30 sailboats, equipped with more than 200 rifles, with seven or eight rifles on each boat, for resisting customs patrols. The reason for using sailboats exclusively is that sailboats travel silently. Customs patrol ships are equipped with listening devices that can detect the sound of distant motorboats. The company also has its own small radio station, which can send and receive telegrams and communicate with smuggling organizations on Taiwan Island. It is scheduled to send a dispatch every three hours. In case of emergency, it will send it at any time, specifically reporting the anchorage of customs patrol ships and the news of their return to port to add coal and water. If it detects that a customs ship is anchored or entering the port to add coal and water, it will immediately dispatch a report to the smuggling organizations on the island and set sail to Quanzhou at any time. Each of these more than 30 sailboats is dispatched every hour or half hour, with each boat loaded with goods waiting to be shipped at any time. If they encounter customs ships along the way, the first ship will be seized, and the subsequent ships can be expected to change course. Moreover, each time a customs ship seizes a boat, it must be escorted back to Xiamen. After the customs ship leaves, the remaining ships will take advantage of the gap to steal through the waves. According to their calculations, if two out of every three ships of goods can pass, they have already broken even, and if they can pass more, they will profit. In addition, they also spend heavily to bribe public officials in the agency. Those who receive their subsidies protect smuggling and transmit news, reporting the specific actions of customs ships and other related news. Therefore, smugglers can receive information quickly and travel unimpeded. The company's general headquarters is located in Tatu, and it also has loading and unloading docks in Shenhu and Xunpu. The land transportation route is divided into Tatu, passing through Hecun, Xuxikeng, and other villages, turning into Kemu, turning west into Anhai, turning north into Zhanglin, Qianpu, turning into Anxi, Nan'an, and other places, and turning east into Shishi. Waterway transportation is unloaded near the river in Quanzhou City, imported into Quanzhou City or transferred to Huian. It is reported that in January of this year, the amount of white sugar smuggled into the country and unloaded near the river in Quanzhou City alone was more than 500 bags, each bag weighing 300 pounds. The Nanshun Trading Company seized in Shishi is far less large-scale than Tatu. Recently, people in the company have been moving to other places, saying that the secret has been leaked and the Quanzhou Pacification Department is paying attention to the investigation. (March 5th)

Garrison Troops in Fujian Province Pursue and Suppress Bandits Who Looted Vehicles; Bandits Occupy the Junction of Minhou, Fuqing, and Yongtai Counties; It is Ascertained that the Bandit Leader Who Looted the Vehicle is Shi Lang 70

Fuzhou Correspondence: Since February 24th, after the long-distance bus on the Fuquan Highway was robbed at Fang Kou, at the junction of Minhou and Fuqing counties, and more than 20 passengers were taken away, the provincial government immediately ordered the Fifth and Tenth Regiments of the Provincial Security Forces to each send two companies, with Zhu Wenbo, the commander of the Fifth Regiment, as the commander, to lead the troops to pursue and suppress the bandits. Up to now, for ten days, the hostages have not been rescued, and the authorities are quite anxious. Until recently, the pursuing and suppressing troops have learned that the bandits are entrenched in Niutou Mountain, at the junction of Minhou, Fuqing, and Yongtai counties. The hostages are held in Chenzhong Ao (晨鐘出), where the defensive works are very solid and equipped with machine guns and other sharp military equipment. Currently, the troops have surrounded and locked the entrances and exits of the two mountains and are attacking on one side. It is expected that there will be fierce battles in the next two or three days. As the bandits are currently busy resisting the army, they have no time to consider the ransom matters. Rumors that each hostage has been priced at 10,000 yuan are likely untrue. As for the bandit leader, Gao Chengxue himself, he is still in Taiwan. The one who orchestrated this vehicle robbery is actually Shi Weigeng, formerly the commander of the pseudo-independent 15th Regiment who harassed the counties of Lianjiang and Luoyuan in eastern Fujian, who has changed his name to Shi Lang. Wei is from Lianjiang and also a graduate of the Fuzhou Private Law and Politics College. He was a classmate of Gao Chengxue. After Wei failed last spring, his troops scattered and his military equipment was lost. He fled to Taiwan, where he met Gao Chengxue. Gao provided him with military equipment, which was smuggled from Taiwan to Fuqing by sailboat. He gathered his own and Gao's former subordinates, and reorganized his forces. Since the discovery of this group of bandits in Fuqing, the atmosphere of banditry has suddenly intensified. The force led by Cai Birong of Dongzhang Town in that county is said to be quite large, calling themselves the Workers' and Peasants' Guerrilla Brigade. Among them, there are many middle school graduates, who serve as false positions such as captains and staff officers, wantonly disturbing the surrounding villages, causing great suffering to the people. Hankou Correspondence: The area bordering Hubei, Henan, Anhui, and Henan in eastern Hubei is the area where Kuang Jixun, Xu Xiangqian, and Xu Haidong, the major bandit groups, are entrenched. Lianghuai Transportation Commissioner Rectifies Salt Tax Revenue; Salt Storage in Bengbu Affects Tax Revenue; Inviting Merchants to Contract for Additional Transportation of Salt 72

Bengbu Correspondence: The Huai salt merchants operating in Bengbu have always taken an average approach. It was once stipulated that the monthly salt storage should be limited to 300,000 market dan, estimating sales for three months. Unexpectedly, in recent years, the transportation merchants with relatively strong capital have suddenly changed the rules, increasing the transportation of salt. Each shipment actually reaches 100,000 market dan, all transported from northern Huai. Currently, the salt stored in the warehouses is more than 700,000 market dan, breaking the equilibrium. Small-capital transportation merchants want to transport more but lack the financial resources, transport less and have no profit to be made. Moreover, the rotation restrictions require them to wait in line and cannot freely compete for sales, making it difficult to wait for a long time. The interest on bank loans and the rent for storing salt in warehouses all increase costs, and the price of salt is invisibly increased. The rotation system has also become stagnant, because old salt has not been sold, and new salt cannot be transported, leading to a sharp decline in tax revenue, which greatly affects the national treasury. Yao Qunyu, the Lianghuai Salt Transportation Commissioner, in order to rectify salt taxes and increase revenue, opened up another path. After submitting a report to the Ministry of Finance and obtaining approval, the additional transportation of salt to the Anhui and Henan shores was contracted out to merchants. The Transportation Office specifically stipulated the amount of tax to be paid to the Anhui and Henan shores. For February of this year, the market tax is 400,000 market dan, that is, out of the 400,000 dan of additional transportation, 360,000 market dan for Bengbu, 32,000 market dan for Mingguang, and 8,000 market dan for Guzhen. The tax payment will be temporarily suspended in March. From April onwards, the amount of tax to be paid each month will be based on the actual sales of the previous month. If the sales in the first month are above 130,000 market dan, then 80,000 market dan of new tax will be paid in the second month, so that at least 50,000 market dan of old tax can be recovered. If the sales are below 130,000 market dan but above 110,000 market dan, at least 45,000 market dan of old tax will be recovered. If the sales are below 110,000 market dan, at least 40,000 market dan of old tax will be recovered. The new and old tax salt stored in Bengbu can be sold throughout the Anhui and Henan shores, and is not limited to the nineteen counties in northern Anhui. The deadline is until the new and old salt stored on the shore is sold to 300,000 market dan (including the salt stored on the shore, in transit, and taxed but not yet transported). During this period, no new sales locations will be opened up on the Anhui and Henan shores, and the current tax payment system will not be changed. When the new salt law is implemented in the future, the government will be responsible for guaranteeing the payment of taxes in advance, and the stored salt will be given the opportunity to be sold first. Before the taxes paid in advance for the stored salt are cleared, the salt transported to the shore according to the new salt law cannot be sold or inserted for sale in advance. When merchants acknowledge the amount, they should pay 2.15 yuan in cash per dan as a guarantee deposit. Once the procedures are completed, the government will immediately transfer the guarantee deposit originally paid by the merchant to the salt tax. This decision to invite merchants to contract will last until the end of January 1937. It is heard that the contracting merchants have recently paid the guarantee deposit to the Banpu Central Bank, and the number of sales is expected to exceed the original 400,000 market dan, which shows the enthusiasm of the merchants to contract. In the future, when the new salt arrives, it will still be sold in rotation, with half new salt and half old salt rotated for sale, in order to be fair and avoid disparity. (March 4th)

Anqing-Hefei Road Accident; Many Deaths and Injuries; Car Overturns at Baisha Bridge in Shucheng; Postal Worker and Soldier Die Instantly 73

Wuhu Correspondence: As of recently, the highways in Anhui Province, including those with paved roads and those with completed earthen roads open to traffic, have reached 3,279 kilometers. Except for the Nanjing-Wuhu line, which was formerly commercially operated but recently reverted to provincial operation due to losses and inability to support it, most other roads are operated by the Provincial Highway Bureau using its own vehicles. However, in terms of business, only the Wuhu-Tunxi road has a slight surplus, while the others barely cover expenses. Unexpectedly, this year, the Nanjing-Wuhu line and the Tunxi-Jingdezhen line have successively experienced tragic accidents in which cars overturned, injuring and killing passengers, and business has become increasingly depressed. Unexpectedly, another accident occurred on the Anqing-Hefei road on the 3rd, resulting in two deaths and seven or eight injuries. The road runs from Anqing through Tongcheng, Shucheng, Taoxi Town, Shangpai River to Hefei, a total length of 110 kilometers, but the road surface is only paved to Shucheng. On the morning of the 3rd, the first bus on the line from Anqing to Shucheng, Anhui Province license plate number 1667, driven by driver He Nvbing, carrying a total of more than 20 passengers, drove to the Baisha Bridge in Shucheng County. Due to the bridge crossing, the horsepower was too great, causing the speed to increase suddenly when descending the bridge. For a moment, the driver could not control it, and the brakes failed, causing it to overturn into the roadside ditch under the bridge. More than a dozen people were injured, and two seriously injured people died instantly. One was a postal worker named Shi Zhiming, 40 years old, from Huaining, who was ordered by the Provincial Postal Bureau to go to the Tianjia'an branch in Huaiyuan to serve, and he brought his wife and two children with him. The other was an unknown soldier. Afterwards, the Shucheng station reported the incident to the Anqing-Hefei Road Traffic Management Office by long-distance telephone. Director Wang hired a doctor to rush to the scene to provide assistance and sent personnel to investigate the cause of the accident, in order to report it to the Construction Department for handling the aftermath. (March 4th)

Songjiang: Severe Spring Cold Causes Damage to Spring Crops 74

Since the beginning of spring, the northwest wind has roared, causing the temperature to drop below zero degrees. The cold penetrates the skin and bones, unseen in decades. Spring crops in the farmland have all been frozen and withered. Small ports on the inland rivers are frozen, and boats have to break the ice to move. Cormorants and ducks are freezing to death every day. The severity of the spring cold can be seen from this.

Fuxing Township Robbery Case Solved, Culprits Escorted to Songjiang 75

Recently, robbery cases have occurred frequently in the eighth district of Punan. The number of bandits is numerous, mostly based in Shuike Ao (水窠為). On the evening of the 28th of last month, at 1 AM, the homes of Zhang Tongsheng and Wu Shouhe, residents of Fuxing Township, were robbed. The bandits fired shots as a warning before leaving. After receiving the report, the county government ordered Fei Gongxia, the captain of the water patrol team, to lead two patrol boats, Tang Shuqin and Shen Shousheng, to investigate and suppress the bandits. On the afternoon of the 1st, in the bamboo garden north of Mapeng, they heard suspicious voices. Fei entered to investigate and saw many people fleeing. He immediately led his team to pursue and caught one person named Zhong A'si, who confessed the names of the fleeing people. Chang Mi (常瞇) escorted Zhong to arrest Tang A'shu, and cotton yarn, cloth, scarves, and other stolen goods were found in his home. His accomplices Nie Boyun and Qi Yincai were subsequently arrested. The bandits all admitted to robbing the Zhang and Wu families in Fuxing Township. There were nineteen accomplices, with two rifles and one matchlock gun. The bandits carrying guns all fled to Shuike Ao. They also confessed to committing multiple robberies. The recovered stolen goods were identified by the victims without error. Fei then escorted Zhong A'si and the other three people and the stolen goods to Songjiang on the 4th, with a document submitted to the county government for review.

Strict General Investigation of Opium and Drug Offenders 76

Regarding the general investigation of opium and drug offenders, the county government convened a meeting of district chiefs at Haishitang on the afternoon of the 4th, chaired by County Magistrate Li. It was decided that the period from March 5th to 15th would be the period of forced investigation. All those who manufacture, sell, or consume drugs, sell opium, smoke privately without a license, as well as those who intend to profit by providing opium or drug smoking in their premises, and those who use limited-term smoking cessation permits to provide smoking to others, those who relapse after compulsory detoxification, those who smuggle and help others smoke, or administer morphine for others, all the above offenders will be included in the scope of the investigation. From the 6th to the 11th, County Magistrate Li, Secretary Shen, and Section Chiefs Huang and Feng will depart for each district to convene township chiefs for training. To promote the general investigation, Guan Yaonan (District 1), Zhu Kongzhao (District 2), Le Fan (District 3), Yang Jingjiang (District 4), Chen Tigun (District 5), Hu Guanxian (District 6), Shen Jizhou (District 7), and Gu Yiru (District 8) were appointed as special commissioners, who were required to go to the countryside on the 6th and complete the report by the 15th. Those who are unable to obtain licenses for smoking will be copied and sent to each district, ordering them to be sent to the county for detoxification in the shortest possible time.

Suzhou: High Court Opens Trial of Young Mistress's Love Affair with Chauffeur 77

Xi Yunqing, the wife of Liu Zirong (i.e., Madame Liu Xi), the son of Liu Huizhi, the former general manager of the Shanghai China Industrial Bank (Xi Yunqing is the daughter of Xi Ehang, a wealthy pigment merchant), had an affair with chauffeur Wu Wenxiang. Liu Zirong found out and had them arrested and sent to the Shanghai District Court. Wu Wenxiang was sentenced to one year and six months in prison. Wu Wenxiang refused to accept the sentence and hired lawyer Dong Banggan to write an appeal to the Jiangsu High Court. After the High Court accepted the case, it summoned Liu Zirong and Liu Xi, and brought Wu Wenxiang, who was in custody, to Suzhou. Yesterday (the 5th) at 10:30 AM, the criminal division judge opened the trial in the first courtroom in Zhicheng. Liu Zirong reported upon being summoned, but Liu Xi did not arrive. Wu Wenxiang hired lawyer Dong Banggan to defend him. First, Wu Wenxiang was interrogated. He testified that in July 1933, he was introduced to the Liu Zirong family to drive a car. In November of the same year, he had an affair with Liu Xi. The reason was that he often sat in the car and slept when he had nothing to do. Liu Xi would come and tell him not to sit in the car but to help in the house. At that time, she would often tell me jokes, which I ignored, intending to stop my business. One day, Liu Zirong drove out and did not return. Liu Xi came to my room, and the first act of adultery occurred. Later, she often came to my room, for more than a year now. After I left the Liu family in May of last year, I never went there again. Liu Xi rented a house in Jixiangfang after going out in July of last year and sent a letter asking me to go, saying that if I didn't go, she would commit suicide, so I went. The money used was Liu Xi's. Later, I wanted to go home, and Liu Xi said that I was ungrateful, etc. Then Liu Zirong was interrogated. He testified that he had been married to Liu Xi for four years and had a child who was three years old this year. On August 2, 1935, Liu Xi left a note and ran away, only a week after Wu Wenxiang ran away. Later, after investigating, he reported to the Public Security Bureau, who arrested them both. At this point, lawyer Dong Banggan stated that Liu Xi had not arrived today, perhaps because she had not received the summons. Liu Xi now lives at 403 Adoyar Road, Shanghai, at her brother Xi Xunde's place. He requested that she be summoned. The judge, seeing that Liu Xi had not arrived, ordered that Liu Xi and Liu Zirong's maids, A Bao and A Jin, be summoned to court again for a scheduled hearing. Liu Zirong was dismissed, and Wu Wenxiang was detained. Because the Xi family is originally from Suzhou, there were many relatives and friends in Suzhou, so many people went to the High Court to listen to the proceedings that day.

Wuxi: Bandits Rob Wealthy Merchant in the Dark of Night 78

Zhang Songnan, a resident of Xiaozhang Lane in Yangxi Township, the third district, is a wealthy merchant in the county who has been engaged in the iron business in Shanghai and Wuxi and has accumulated some savings. Unexpectedly, he was targeted by bandits. At about 1 AM on the morning of the 4th, more than a dozen bandits disguised as workers, holding iron rulers, wooden sticks, slings, and other weapons, climbed over the walls and broke into the house, directly entering the rooms to search and ransack. After about an hour, they left with a roar. After checking the items, it was found that more than thirty pieces of clothing, various valuable gold ornaments, more than twenty stones of white rice, and cash were stolen, totaling more than 500 yuan in losses. The victim immediately reported the incident to the eighth branch of the Public Security Bureau in charge, requesting the apprehension of the stolen goods and bandits.

After receiving the order, the Public Security Bureau of this county immediately made active preparations. They practice at the Ximen Sports Field every day at 8 AM and 2 PM, in preparation for the inspection.

Jiaxing: Verdict in the Case of the Abuse and Death of a Maid 83

The Zhou Lu family in Jiaxing Yangguan Street was reported by neighbors for beating the maid Dong Lan (14 years old) to death. The Zhen Township Office and the Public Security Bureau ordered the police to arrest Zhou Lu and send her to the District Court Procuratorate for investigation. The prosecutor led officials to the barren tomb of Qiujing Bridge to open the coffin and examine the maid's body. The examination revealed that the body was injured all over. After investigation, the family was prosecuted for intentional injury, abandonment resulting in death, and deprivation of freedom. The criminal court judge Feng Zhaohuang summoned the witnesses and interrogated her repeatedly. At 5 PM on the afternoon of the 4th, the verdict was announced. The main text stated that Zhou Lu, for a person without the ability to save themselves, did not provide the assistance necessary for their survival, resulting in death, and was sentenced to three years and six months of imprisonment. For placing a person in a non-free position similar to slavery, a sentence of one year of imprisonment was issued. The sentence was fixed at four years. The related civil lawsuit portion was transferred to the Civil Division of this court for trial.

Exemption from Surcharges and Fines for Arrears in Land Tax 84

The old arrears in land tax in Jiaxing amounted to more than one million yuan. Although the provincial department has sent commissioners to urge payment, there has been no improvement. The Finance Department has now drafted a method for clearing the arrears, dividing it into stages. In order to show consideration for the farmers, it has been specifically determined that for all grain households with arrears from 1927 to 1935, if they voluntarily submit to the treasury to clear all previous years' grain taxes during the first clearing period (i.e., from March 1st to the end of May), the surcharges and fines for late payment of land tax will be exempted. The county has been ordered to comply. In addition to announcing this to all businesses, the county government has also instructed the collection personnel of the Jiaxing and Xiushui offices to be informed. If payment is not completed by the deadline, penalties will be added, and arrests and detentions will be carried out to pursue payment.

Rice Shortage and Rising Market Prices 86

Hangzhou's rice supply has always relied on rice boats from Hushu to purchase and supply from various places. Recently, due to the severe cold weather, there has been a shortage of goods, causing the market to continue to rise. From the 5th, rice stores in the city raised the price of No. 1 to No. 4 pointed rice and high-grade steamed grain by 40 cents per stone, and No. 5 pointed rice and secondary rice by 60 cents per stone. Fragrant japonica late rice was raised by 20 cents per stone. This was announced and implemented by the Rice Price Appraisal Committee.

Since the Hangzhou Money Industry Joint Reserve has been actively preparing, everything is now ready. It was officially established on the 5th. The procedures for clearing and exchanging are generally the same as those of the bank reserve. The Central Bank, Bank of China, Bank of Communications, and Farmers Bank have been specially contracted as banks with the reserve. Except for the Farmers Bank, which has already negotiated the various procedures, the other three banks are still in negotiations due to the interest rate issue. As of yesterday, the Qianzhuang(錢莊) which had paid reserve funds to the banks designated by the reserve included Yichang Yuantai, Taisheng, Shunchang, etc., totaling more than 200,000.

Xiaoshan: Extreme Cold in Xiaoshan Causes Many Deaths 88

The cold air in Xiaoshan last winter was slightly weaker, but after the spring equinox, the cold became severe. It is now mid-spring, and it should be warm and breezy, with flowers and trees blooming. Unexpectedly, it has recently been forced by cold air from the north, even more severe than in winter. The thermometer is two degrees Celsius below zero. Water freezes in the morning and does not melt at noon. This kind of spring cold only occurred at the end of the Guangxu period, so it is an unusual cold that has not been seen in more than thirty years. Two or three beggars and coolies are freezing to death along the way every day. The city's free coffin association has run out of coffins, and the supply cannot meet the demand.

Method for Collecting Education Savings 89

The Education Bureau of this county believes that the primary school fund is unavailable, making it difficult for schools to operate. To ensure stable education funding in the future, it has drafted a method and submitted it to the Education Department for approval. At the principals' service promotion meeting on the 2nd of this month, the method was distributed to the principals of each primary school for compliance. It will be implemented from the first semester of the 25th year for a period of ten years. Each semester, elementary students should pay 10 cents, senior students should pay 20 cents, and teachers and staff should pay 1 yuan per person per semester. However, those with a monthly salary of less than 10 yuan and poor family conditions may be exempted at discretion. It will be implemented in 1936 in order to accumulate funds that will be completed after ten years to become a permanent fund.

Discovery of Spring Plague, Deaths Common 90

In the area of Jinxi Bridge Pengjia Village in Pan Right Township under the county's jurisdiction, a spring plague has recently been discovered due to the unusually cold weather. Those who suffer from this epidemic first develop a fever, then become dizzy and die after more than ten hours. To date, the number of deaths has reached more than thirty people. All residents of the village are panicking due to fear of the epidemic. In view of the prevalence of the epidemic, the county government has specially hired Chinese and Western doctors to investigate the village to determine what disease it is, and has ordered that appropriate treatment and prevention methods be implemented to prevent it from spreading.

Record of the Loan Committee Meeting - Approved Loans of Over 37,900 Yuan - Applicants Still Eager, Hope They Will Not Overreport Capital 92

The Shanghai Industry and Commerce Loan Review Committee held its 24th decision-making meeting at the Bank of China National Products Building at 4:30 PM on the 4th. Committee members present included Cai Zengji, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Zhang Peishen, Song Ziliang, Yu Zuoting, Wang Xiaolai (Yu as proxy), Chen Guangfu (Bei as proxy), etc. Chairman Cai Zengji reported on routine daily affairs. Sixty-one applications for small credit loans were submitted. After review, it was decided that one application would be approved as is, eight would be approved for half the originally requested amount, and forty-seven would have a portion of the loan amount reduced. A total of 37,950 yuan was approved for loans. Eight other applications were rejected either because the business activities did not conform to the loan principles, or because the intended use of the loan was inconsistent with the regulations. All reviewed cases will be individually notified to the applicants for their information. It was also reported that there has been a large number of requests for application forms recently. However, many applicants still overreport their capital and do not comply with the rule that loans cannot exceed half of the capital. It was decided at yesterday's meeting that any such cases in the future will be rejected without investigation. It is hoped that companies needing loans will inquire about the procedures in detail at the committee's office when requesting forms to avoid repeating errors.

Special District Telephone Issue Committee - Submits Petition to the Municipal Government for Negotiation - Requests Consideration of Public Sentiment and Prompt Negotiation with the Municipal Council - To Repeal the Telephone Company's Concession Contract 95

The Special District Telephone Issue Committee, in order to implement its opposition to price increases, specifically submitted a petition to the Municipal Government yesterday, requesting it to initiate serious negotiations with the Municipal Council, hoping to find a satisfactory solution. The original text of the petition is extracted below: The petition is for the matter of requesting consideration. Since the issue of the Shanghai Telephone Company's price increase arose, the news has spread, causing widespread unrest throughout the city. Difficulties were voiced to the Municipal Council Board of Directors, requesting ways to stop it. However, the Municipal Council, based on the signed concession contract, approved its annual interest rate of one percent, disregarding the current state of Shanghai's commerce and prosperity. It is noted that telephone service is a public utility. During this time of social and economic collapse, the spirit of mutual assistance should be upheld to benefit both people and businesses, in order to seek a way of mutual existence and operation. If the hardships of commerce are ignored, relying on the contract as a shield, and exploitation is pursued as a goal, and if the city's economic recession continues unabated, and businesses cannot bear the burden, then all are bound to perish together. Since the Special District Telephone implemented the new system on March 1, limiting commercial telephones to 150 calls per month and residential telephones to 100 calls per month, the businesses in the city are groaning in agony, which is no different from putting our industry and commerce in a hopeless situation. According to the statistics of the affiliated associations, under the old system, the cost of commercial telephone usage was more than 13 yuan, with an average of 20 calls. Now, under the new system, the cost is 10 yuan, limited to 150 calls per month. For those who exceed this number, a fee of 3 cents is charged per call. Currently, there are more than 48,600 telephone subscribers in the Special District, which means a monthly loss of more than 486,000 yuan in national currency. Calculated annually, the number is shocking. The affiliated associations, entrusted by various public bodies in the city, are deeply concerned about this issue and have no solution. In addition to petitioning the central government to request evaluation and recovery for self-operation, a special petition is submitted to Your Excellency, earnestly requesting consideration of public sentiment and prompt negotiation with the Municipal Council, demanding the repeal of the Shanghai Telephone Company's concession contract, and accepting the requests of all subscribers: increasing the basic number of calls, increasing commercial telephones to 333 calls, and residential telephones to 217 calls, installing meters, stipulating a three-month trial period, and eliminating communication fees in the Chinese Concession. The above requests are truly for the benefit of the people and are hoped for by the general public. Earnestly request review and approval, and prompt negotiation with the Municipal Council, hoping to find a satisfactory solution. Then the citizens will feel the same great kindness. Respectfully submitted to Wu, Mayor of Shanghai.

Unified Bonds Printed - Exchange and Redemption to Begin on the 11th - Deadline is June 30 - Exchange Offices Have Posted Announcements 96

The Ministry of Finance, in order to reorganize domestic public bonds and treasury certificates, submitted the proposal to the Central Political Conference, which was passed, to issue 146 million yuan in Unified Public Bonds, stipulating that starting from the 11th of this month, exchange and redemption would be carried out by the Bond Exchange Office at 452 Jiangxi Road in this city and the three Central China Communications Banks in various locations. It is learned that the bonds have already been printed and are being stamped and sealed for timely issuance. The details are noted as follows:

Divided into Five Types for Scheduled Exchange and Redemption

The Unified Public Bonds are divided into five types: Type A bonds are scheduled to begin exchange and redemption on March 11, including six types: the 22nd Year Patriotic Treasury Bonds, Short-Term Treasury Certificates, 18th Year Customs Duty Treasury Bonds, 22nd Year North China War Zone Public Bonds, Security Public Bonds, and 19th Year Customs Duty Treasury Bonds. Type B bonds are scheduled to begin exchange and redemption on March 21, including five types: the 19th Year Rehabilitation Treasury Bonds, 24th Year Treasury Bonds, 24th Year Sichuan Financial Reorganization Treasury Bonds, 23rd Year Customs Duty Treasury Bonds, and 20th Year Cigarette Tax Treasury Bonds. Type C bonds are scheduled to begin exchange and redemption on April 1, including seven types: the 18th Year Compilation and Omission Treasury Bonds, 20th Year Consolidated Tax Treasury Bonds, 20th Year Financial Short-Term Public Bonds, 20th Year Salt Tax Treasury Bonds, 20th Year Jiangsu-Zhejiang Silk Industry Public Bonds, 18th Year Disaster Relief Public Bonds, Military Needs Public Bonds, 18th Year Troop Reduction Public Bonds, and 20th Year Customs Duty Treasury Bonds. Type D bonds are scheduled to begin exchange and redemption on April 11, including eight types: the 19th Year Customs Duty Public Bonds, 7-Year 6% Public Bonds, 20th Year Disaster Relief Public Bonds, Italian Boxer Indemnity Certificates, 24th Year Financial Public Bonds, 23rd Year Customs Duty Public Bonds, Russian Indemnity Certificates, and Consolidated Tax Certificates. Type E bonds are scheduled to begin exchange and redemption on April 21, including five types: the 22nd Year Customs Duty Treasury Bonds, 24th Year Flood Relief and Public Works Bonds, Reorganized 7% Public Bonds, Reorganized 6% Public Bonds, and 15th Year Spring Festival Treasury Bonds.

New Tickets Printed and Stamped

Exchange and redemption of bonds has been designated to be handled by the Bond Exchange Office at 452 Jiangxi Road in this city, and the three Central, China, and Communications Banks in various locations. An exchange application form has now been printed for bondholders to request, fill out, and submit within the exchange period to obtain a temporary receipt. After five days, they can return to exchange for the bonds. The bonds are divided into several denominations: 5,000 yuan, 1,000 yuan, 100 yuan, and 10 yuan. Bondholders can calculate the total amount and fill out the application form indicating the denominations and number of bonds to be exchanged. If the remainder is less than 10 yuan, it will be calculated at 98% of its value to make up a full 10 yuan for exchange. If the remainder is less than 1 yuan, the exchange office will provide stamp tax tickets at 98% of its value. The new public bonds have already been printed and sent to the exchange office for stamping and sealing to prepare for timely issuance. Bondholders can immediately go to request application forms, fill them out, and go to exchange for the bonds on schedule.

Exchange Office Posts Announcement from the Ministry of Finance

The bond exchange office posted an announcement stating: By order of the Ministry of Finance, Public Decree No. 22820, it is stated that according to the Revised Bond Schedule Case in February of the 21st year of the Republic of China, the various bonds that should be exchanged for new bonds or have interest coupons added have been exchanged in order. It has been four years, and there are not many remaining bonds that have not been exchanged. This time, the issuance of Unified Public Bonds to exchange old bonds has been stipulated to begin on March 11, 25th year of the Republic of China, and end on June 30. All old bonds for which new bonds are exchanged or interest coupons are added should be uniformly terminated on March 10, 25th year of the Republic of China. After that, Unified Public Bonds will be directly exchanged for old bonds to simplify the process. In addition to the public announcement and distribution, a copy of the announcement is urgently issued for the office to follow and handle. At the time of the deadline, a detailed list of the various bonds and the numbers of interest coupons that should be issued, have been issued, and have not been issued, should be reported to the ministry for record. This order, etc. Therefore, it is hereby announced, hoping that bondholders will check and handle accordingly.

The City Slightly Warmer Yesterday - The Consecutive Days of Spring Cold are Rare in Forty-One Years 99

Since the city became very cold on the 2nd of this month, all the ditches, tap water pipes, and inland rivers in various places remained frozen until yesterday morning. The lowest temperature was 26.1 degrees. Only after 1 PM did the thawing gradually begin, and after 2 PM, it was completely thawed. Sailing gradually resumed, and the prices of vegetables, coal, and other goods gradually stabilized. However, because the wind direction was still from the northeast, it was difficult to rise to between 40 and 50 degrees for the time being.

A Phenomenon Not Seen in Forty-One Years

A reporter from the East China News Agency learned from astronomical circles that the severe cold in the city was a record not seen in forty-one years. In 1895 (i.e., the 21st year of the Guangxu reign of the Qing Dynasty), on March 16, due to all-day spring snow, the temperature suddenly dropped to a minimum of 21.6 degrees and a maximum of 32.7 degrees, and it did not thaw all day. Even eggs were frozen and cracked. Since then, there has never been such severe cold in the past forty-one years. It is also learned that the Siberian high pressure has recently been hovering at 780 millimeters, hence this phenomenon.

Japanese Newspaper Reports No Immediate Warming

The Japanese-language Shanghai Daily reported that the recent cold weather has resulted in daily reports of deaths from freezing. According to the Shanghai Observatory, the current cold air will continue. The low pressure today is in the north and south of Okinawa and at the mouth of Wonsan, Korea. Because the low pressure south of Okinawa is moving strongly eastward, the high pressure is gradually weakening, so the low pressure is being moderated, and the cold air will not go away immediately.

Shin Hwa and Other Factories Face Supply Shortages Due to Lack of Raw Materials 100

According to Central News Agency, Shin Hwa Textile Mills, including the seven mills in Shanghai, experienced debt disputes due to a shortage of working capital during last year's industrial recession. Fortunately, they were able to overcome the difficulties. Immediately afterwards, an improvement committee was formed to focus on reorganization. Now, all the spindles are gradually being replaced with new ones. The products are of high quality and sales are brisk. However, due to a lack of raw materials, they still cannot produce at full capacity. A report was recently published stating that the Bank of China was investing in the takeover, but this has been denied by the factory. The following is an examination of its recent production situation:

Replacing Machines to Increase Efficiency

Shin Hwa Textile Mills has a total of nine mills. In addition to the three mills located in Wuxi and the four mills located in Hankou, the rest are located in Shanghai. It has a total of 529,780 spindles, 43,940 yarn machines, and 4,861 looms. Since the establishment of the improvement committee last year, it has focused on reorganization and innovation, replacing new machinery and adding spinning machines, investing 1.67 million yuan to convert all machinery to the 1934 model. The organization and management of the factory are also striving for rationalization.

Factories Two and Five Remain Closed

The factory's business last year saw improved product quality and strong sales due to improvements in production methods. The daily output was 800 bales of yarn (420 pounds per bale) and 15,000 bolts of various fabrics (40 yards per bolt). However, due to the smaller cotton yield this year, which is only 70% of last year's, there is a lack of abundant raw materials for production. Therefore, factories two and five in Shanghai are currently closed. It is reported that the factory's products for April, May, and June of this year have already been completely pre-ordered and sold out.

Industrial Circles Hope for Assistance from All Parties

According to industry representatives, China's production industry is gradually progressing, but requires assistance from all parties and joint efforts. In terms of raw materials, taking raw cotton as an example, the quality of domestic production must be improved and the output must be increased by more than double. It is hoped that the government will earnestly promote and guide this point. In terms of financial assistance, in the flour milling industry, the domestic wheat production is only sufficient for four or five months of use by flour mills nationwide, so it is also necessary to promote improvement. With abundant raw materials and excellent machinery, it is hoped that the banking industry can provide convenient financial assistance. Then industrial development and the national economy can be revitalized.

The Two Railways Compiled and Printed a Goods Classification and Easy Inspection Table - An Essential Tool for Calculating Railway Freight 106

The Traffic Department of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways, in order to facilitate merchants' inspection of goods classification when reporting freight, specifically compiled an easy inspection table by arranging the Ministry of Railways' sixth edition of the General Goods Classification Table in the order of the number of strokes. At the beginning of the table, there are four types of indexes: number of strokes, radical, four-corner code, and Mandarin Romanization spelling. For any goods that the Ministry of Railways has classified, the category can be found in the easy inspection table within half a minute, which is very convenient. At the end of the table, there are nine types of documents related to freight rates, such as the price list and the list of goods names, which are all complete. All merchants who report freight on the railway should have one copy for reference. This book has already been published and is available for sale at the Business Section of the Traffic Department of the Shanghai North Station, the Model Book Stall at the station, the No. 1 Business Office of the Two Railways at 407 Jing'an Temple Road, the No. 2 Business Office of the Two Railways at 18 Waima Road outside the Sixteen Pups in the Nanshi, and the Business Office of the Two Railways at 327 Zhongshi Road, Taiping Road, Nanjing. It is said that each book only costs 4 jiao in national currency for printing costs.

Announcement from the Cotton Industry Control Association: Clause Regarding Moisture Content on Cotton Transaction Forms 107

The Cotton Industry Control Committee has recently issued a notification to all cotton industry organizations under the document number 統字 third six three six, stating: "Approved is a letter from the Central Cotton Adulteration and Water Mixing Elimination Office, which stated, 'Upon investigation of Article 7 of the Provisional Regulations for Eliminating Cotton Adulteration and Water Mixing, it is stipulated that if a yarn factory purchases cotton and encounters moisture content exceeding the standard but not exceeding the maximum limit, the price should be deducted accordingly. If the moisture content is below the standard, compensation should be made accordingly.' Thus, for cotton purchases, if the moisture content is between 11% and 13%, the price should indeed be deducted based on the moisture content. If the moisture content is below 11%, compensation should also be made. Currently, although various factories determine the price based on the level of moisture content when purchasing cotton, the transaction forms do not specify the deduction and compensation methods. This often leads sellers to believe that only price deductions occur, without any increases, making them unwilling to sell dry raw materials, which significantly impacts the elimination policy. It is proposed that your association notify the China Cotton Industry Joint Association, consult with the Yarn Factory Joint Association, and the Japanese Textile Industry Association in China, so that in the future, when purchasing cotton, they must indicate the moisture content in the 'Moisture Content' column on the transaction form and deduct or compensate the price according to Article 7 of the Elimination Regulations to ensure fairness and prevent excuses. Therefore, we should report this matter and respectfully request your review and compliance.'" Upon review, the method proposed by the office to indicate on the cotton purchase transaction form, in the moisture content column, "Moisture content should be deducted or compensated according to Article 7 of the Elimination Regulations," stating that yarn factories should deduct the price for cotton with moisture content exceeding the standard but not exceeding the maximum limit and compensate for cotton with moisture content below the standard, is beneficial to both buyers and sellers of cotton. It is hereby requested that you investigate, inform the industry to diligently indicate the proposed wording on the transaction forms to ensure fairness.

Announcement by the International Trade Bureau: Reasons for Last Year's Sudden Increase in Tung Oil Sales and Five Fundamental Ways to Improve Tung Oil 108

Last year, China's tung oil exports were very brisk. The market price reached a high of eighty-five yuan per picul, which was rare in recent years. However, domestic consumption decreased significantly due to the weak purchasing power of the people. In total, last year's tung oil exports amounted to 738,865 metric tons, an increase of 86,029 metric tons or 11% compared to the previous year, with a value of 41,582,879 yuan, ranking first among last year's exports and worthy of attention. The following is a record of the statistics released by the International Trade Bureau and the reasons for the sudden increase in sales:

Quantities Exported to Various Countries Last Year

Last year, the largest quantity of tung oil exports went to the United States, accounting for 60% to 70% of the total. Other countries accounted for only 30%. The United States imported 491,999 piculs, worth 28,057,248 yuan; Hong Kong 87,481 piculs, worth 4,129,109 yuan; the United Kingdom 36,551 piculs, worth 2,117,974 yuan; Germany 28,933 piculs, worth 1,787,412 yuan; France 31,154 piculs, worth 1,778,769 yuan; the Netherlands 20,607 piculs, worth 1,261,417 yuan; Denmark 7,960 piculs, worth 478,242 yuan; Japan 7,893 piculs, worth 361,867 yuan; Italy 5,382 piculs, worth 328,126 yuan; Sweden 4,340 piculs, worth 286,667 yuan; Norway 4,575 piculs, worth 277,519 yuan; Austria 3,590 piculs, worth 235,925 yuan; Belgium 2,885 piculs, worth 164,868 yuan; Argentina 1,262 piculs, worth 83,801 yuan; Kwantung Leased Territory 1,020 piculs, worth 41,787 yuan; India 541 piculs, worth 39,950 yuan; Finland 504 piculs, worth 31,785 yuan; Canada 197 piculs, worth 19,105 yuan; and other countries 1,981 piculs, worth 101,308 yuan; totaling 738,865 piculs, worth 41,582,879 yuan.

Tung Oil Merchants All Made Significant Profits

Last year, the harvests of tung seeds in Hunan, Sichuan, Hubei, Shaanxi, Zhejiang, and Anhui were abundant, and the oil content was also very good. The market price of tung seeds was 19 yuan per picul, which was 7 yuan higher than the previous year. Each picul of tung oil required 224 catties of tung seeds, so the cost of each picul of tung oil was at least 41 yuan. Merchants engaged in tung oil exports, whether in the producing areas, Hankou, or Shanghai, made significant profits last year. However, due to the small amount of inventory, they were unable to fully supply the needs of foreign countries, so the profits they earned were not fully satisfied.

Three Reasons for the Sudden Increase in Sales

As for the reasons why tung oil trade suddenly became popular last year, there are approximately the following points: The United States is the largest market for China's tung oil, with average annual imports reaching 120 million pounds. After the economic panic, this decreased to 70 to 80 million pounds. In recent years, due to the implementation of the economic recovery plan, significant achievements have been made, and various industries have gradually recovered. The demand for tung oil has gradually returned to normal, so China's tung oil sales to the United States have also increased. After the outbreak of the Italian-Ethiopian War, there were concerns about the interruption of traffic in the Mediterranean. European countries actively stockpiled raw materials as a precaution, and tung oil, as one of the most important raw materials, experienced increased demand. China's tung oil production is scattered inland, and the transportation and sales of goods are very complicated. Once demand increases sharply, the market inventory is exhausted, and supply cannot be sustained, so prices increase accordingly. From the above, it can be seen that the main reason for the prosperity of China's tung oil exports last year was the sharp increase in overseas demand. The reason for the price increase was that last year, although China's tung oil exports were prosperous, this phenomenon was only a temporary result of supply not meeting demand, rather than China's tung oil having the ability to expand sales in overseas markets. It is difficult to regard this as a normal development.

Improvements Needed to Maintain Permanence

Therefore, if we want to maintain the permanent prosperity of tung oil exports, we still need to fundamentally improve the production and sales of tung oil. The most important areas for improvement are the following five points: China's tung oil cultivation methods are extremely rudimentary. After purchasing the tung seeds, the oil presses store them at will, which inevitably leads to spoilage. The oil extraction methods are also very outdated, so the quality is poor, the color is uneven, the impurities cannot be completely removed, the oil residue is too heavy, and the acidity is too high. Moreover, because oil extraction is a manual industry, it is difficult to maintain consistent quality. China's oil extraction adheres to old methods, so the oil extraction rate is extremely low. The amount of oil lost each year across the country is astonishing. The transportation and sales procedures are extremely complicated, and some merchants mix in adulterated oil in order to seek exorbitant profits, which degrades the quality and affects foreign credibility. Although the commodity inspection bureaus of various ports have recently set qualified standards, the standards are lower than those in the United States. This should be gradually raised. The packaging and transportation methods are poor, the transportation costs are high, and there are occasional interruptions, which often prevent timely delivery, so there is a risk of supply not meeting demand in the market. Tung oil exports are entirely in the hands of foreign firms. There is no domestic organization directly engaged in tung oil exports, and oil merchants cannot coordinate with each other, so market prices are entirely controlled by foreigners.

The United States Cannot Currently Meet Its Own Needs

Tung oil is one of China's specialty products and often has a monopoly in the international market. Although the United States is also engaged in tung tree planting, it cannot currently meet its own needs. If we can seize the opportunity, quickly make improvements, and establish international credibility, then the future will be bright. The most important areas for improvement are production, manufacturing, transportation, and sales. In terms of production, we should first concentrate China's tung tree planting and provide government assistance to engage in large-scale planting. Scientific methods can be used, the variety can be unified, the output can be calculated, and production can be increased. In terms of manufacturing, new oil extraction methods should be actively adopted to increase the oil extraction rate. At the same time, attention should be paid to refining and separating the oil into grades, and establishing standards for each grade. In terms of transportation, economical packaging and transportation methods should be researched, and transportation companies should also find ways to reduce freight costs and implement responsible transportation to achieve economic efficiency and convenience. As for trade, the fundamental goal is to concentrate exports. If domestic tung oil merchants can unite and form a large-scale export organization with common strength, then China's foreign tung oil market can be gradually consolidated.

Subsidy for Puji Sanatorium: Municipal Government Approves Subsidy of 20,000 Yuan Annually 113

The Shanghai Puji Sanatorium was founded by philanthropist Lu Bohong. The sanatorium is located south of Beiqiao in Shanghai County and is designed and built according to the latest European and American hospital standards. It specializes in admitting patients with mental illnesses and is divided into male and female wards, with four houses in each ward, totaling eight houses, which can accommodate more than 600 people. The location is quiet, the air is fresh, and specialized doctors from Europe and the United States are hired to provide diagnosis and treatment. It opened on June 29 last year, and has since admitted a large number of inpatients. The sanatorium previously applied to the municipal government for a subsidy for annual expenses, and was approved by the municipal government on the 3rd of this month to allocate an annual subsidy of 20,000 yuan.

According to information from the two railway bureaus, the plum blossom viewing trip designed by the bureau was originally scheduled from February 25 to March 8. Frozen Fish Merchants Petition the Ministry of Industry: Please Maintain State-Run Fish Markets; Do Not Change the Original Intention Due to Resistance from Fishmongers; Hoping that the Fishing Industry Can Recover 118

The Dagong News Agency reports that the ice-fresh fish merchants of this city, in order to request the maintenance of the state-run principle of fish markets and oppose joint government-business operations, have submitted a petition to the Ministry of Industry through Xu Yifei and others from the Ice-Fresh Fish Merchants Public Welfare Association, stating: "To petition for the matter. Shanghai is a major port in the Southeast and a commercial center. The establishment of a fish market to regulate the economy and balance production and sales is indeed an essential plan to remedy shortcomings and correct abuses. All our fish merchants and fishermen are happy, believing that they can be freed from the constraints and exploitations of fishmongers, and that the suffering of manipulation and exploitation can be permanently eliminated. Therefore, we eagerly await its realization, no different from hoping for rain during a severe drought. However, recent rumors and reports in the newspapers indicate that the Ministry, because fishmongers are resistant to complying, has allowed them to remain at their original location and change to fish market brokers, and to establish a branch market at the 16th Pier, which means that fishmongers have invested 500,000 yuan, changing state-run operations to joint government-business operations. In addition to the original commissions, they are also allowed to charge an additional 1% or 2% commission from merchants or vendors to increase the revenue of the fish market. The rumors are rife. Although we dare not make presumptuous judgments, the rumors are enough to cause our merchants to be alarmed. It is said that laws should not be changed unless there are ten benefits, and systems should not be changed unless there are ten harms. The fish market as a state-run enterprise has long been determined and is known to all. If it is suddenly changed to a joint government-business operation due to the stubbornness of the fishmongers, it will not only damage the credibility of the government, but the common disease of merchants, who only seek private gain and disregard the overall situation, will become even more unscrupulous and intensify their malpractice. In the end, the people will be burdened more heavily than Mount Tong, even though the country is not yet well-governed. Furthermore, since the fishmongers themselves have reached the end of their strength, how can they have the ability to invest? It is nothing more than a stopgap measure. Thus, the disadvantages of joint government-business operations are so great and unprofitable, and the possibility of successful joint operations is so remote. Maintaining the original agreement is acceptable, but mixing government and business is unacceptable. This is one reason why merchants are alarmed by the proposed change. We were hoping that the opening of the fish market would sweep away the accumulated abuses of the past, but who knew that the old problems would not be eliminated, and the idea of adding commissions would arise again? The fishmongers are being generous at other people's expense, but the merchants are unable to afford it. It is like a flock of sparrows chirping repeatedly that it is impossible. This is another reason why merchants are alarmed by the addition of commissions. The matter concerns our vital interests, and it is difficult to remain silent. Therefore, we have submitted this direct report, hoping that Your Excellency will make a decisive judgment and not change the original intention of state-run operations due to the fishmongers' resistance, so that the burden can be reduced and there is hope for the revival of the fishing industry. We present this report in fear and trembling, hoping for your consideration. Respectfully submitted to Wu of the Ministry of Industry, Xu Yifei and others from the Shanghai Ice-Fresh Fish Merchants Association."

Shen Ju, a local woman currently residing at No. 46 Yuru Lane, Tianhou Palace Bridge, age twenty-three, joined a song and dance troupe in 1930 and went to Beijing to perform.
