Drama 212

Insect Sound Society Traffic (1300) 5:30 PM to 7:00 PM

Characters Broadcasters

Lin Zeqi ...... Wu Du

Bai Qiuying ...... Qian Jing

Li Qianqing ...... Sun Lian

Miss Chen ...... Xiao Zhu

Zheng Xiangquan: Lu Jing

Characters Broadcasters

Drinker A ...... Han Bai

Drinker B ...... Ru Ming

Drinker C ...... Tuo Xin

Coffee Shop Owner ...... Lu Jun

We all know... How painful and embarrassing it would be if someone forced us to shake hands with our enemies!

The pain of Da Sheng Lin Zeqi being forced by his father to marry a woman he does not love is also imaginable. He wanted to use his strength to resist, but he knew that his father's idea was completely influenced by his stepmother, and his father was also innocent. This situation extinguished his bursting courage. However, how embarrassing it was for him!

He felt like he was traveling alone in the middle of a vast desert: He didn't know when the yellow sand would come; He didn't know when a big eagle would fly by; He didn't know when a horse thief would attack; He didn't know when the water in the bottle would run dry. All around him was desolate and lonely. Looking behind, he didn't know where his hometown was; Looking ahead, he didn't know where the foreign country was. If the water in his bottle ran dry and he was extremely thirsty, if another traveler suddenly met him at this time and gave him a drink of cool water, how grateful and tearful would he be? But this kind of traveler is not easy to find.

Loneliness, desolation, loneliness, panic, filled his entire heart. Therefore, he could only waste his youthful time in a coffee shop.

Bai Qiuying, a coffee shop waitress, was a young woman who was also forced out of her family's small desert and escaped to this large desert of society. However, she had a great expectation, hoping that her missing lover, Li Qianqing, would come to find her one day. For this reason, although she had suffered the insults and deceptions of those frivolous guests, she always endured it and never complained to anyone.

It was a late night in early winter. The fire in the coffee shop was still burning so brightly, but most of the guests had dispersed and left reluctantly. The only one who was reluctant to leave was Lin Zeqi. He wanted to use whiskey to numb his wounded heart. The theater behind closed, and a group of customers walked in amid laughter. When Bai Qiuying went to greet them, she discovered the hope she had endured and waited for so bitterly for several years – her lover, Li Qianqing. With a heart full of enthusiasm and joy, she called out to her lover. She wanted to pour out all the difficulties and hardships she had endured over the years in her lover's arms. Who knew that the reality was completely unexpected: Li Qianqing had already completely forgotten her and had fallen in love with someone else. He originally wanted to completely ignore her, recognizing her as a complete stranger. But he also thought that he had written her many love letters and taken a photo of the two of them holding hands. Bai Qiuying might use these things to announce his crimes and break up his marriage with his new love. Therefore, he had to tempt her with money. He took out a thousand dollars to buy back the letters and photos he had written to her.

This situation made Lin Zeqi in the next seat unable to bear it any longer. He told Bai Qiuying not to take his money; She did not have to return those evidences to him; And that he should announce his many crimes to the community, to punish those unkind people. However, Bai Qiuying only said with tears in her eyes: "I forgive him, you also forgive him!" She returned all the letters and photos to him; She threw the whole thousand green and red banknotes into the burning charcoal basin without any stinginess, and a burst of brilliant sparks rose in the charcoal basin.

Li Qianqing's business was done, and he left impatiently.

Because Lin Zeqi came here every day, Bai Qiuying already had a very harmonious relationship with him. Lin Zeqi had told Bai Qiuying about his own pain; Bai Qiuying had also told Lin Zeqi about her own sadness. They already had a sympathetic heart to each other. After this stimulus, they became even more deeply aware of each other. In the world, only hungry people sympathize with hungry people; Only disappointed people sympathize with disappointed people; Finally, they joined hands, like lonely travelers in the desert who met an eternal companion, no longer lonely; Nor is there any more panic. As Lin Zeqi said: "With this pair of travelers in the desert, the yellow sand will cover

Page 18

Page 19

Wei; The eagle will turn into a yellow oriole; The horse thief will turn into a knight of the Middle Ages; Everywhere there will be green springs when we are thirsty. What else do we have to worry about or fear!" (The End)

Pingtan 213

Lu Qiuxia's Double Pearl Phoenix

Sino-Western (1040) 7:00 PM to 8:00 PM

Opening "New Daiyu Burying Flowers"

A beautiful woman in Xiaoxiang Pavilion,

Sick and sad, her heart grieves.

She cherishes the beauty of the flowers on the branches,

And gets up early in spring to busily dress.

She orders the maid to insert them on the branches,

And to protect them from sparrows.

But the heavens always work against her,

With frequent heavy rains and raging winds.

They destroy the thousands of red and purple blooms,

Leaving the trees without fragrance.

It is like a beautiful woman encountering misfortune,

Her beauty fades and her life is short.

The Xiaoxiang Fairy is extremely sentimental,

And her heart breaks when she sees the scene.

She thinks that her delicate body is like a flower,

But she often suffers from illnesses like encountering a storm.

She suddenly has a feeling of shared suffering,

So she carries a hoe to the tree and builds a beautiful tomb to bury the petals.

She mourns and weeps before the grave,

Her sad and painful tears soaking her clothes.

It is beyond her power to turn back the tide, and she hates it.

Because it is difficult to find an immortality pill in the world,

And there is no resurrection fragrance.

Today I bury the withered flowers,

Who will bury me one day?

Thinking of this, her heart aches again,

And she bids farewell to the tomb and returns to Xiaoxiang.

When her burning manuscripts scatter her fragrant soul in the future,

Like falling flowers, she drifts to the vast wilderness.

Although the beautiful woman dies, her name will be remembered.

Several Singers Performing at the Jin Cheng Stage 216

— Bai Yun

Tianyi's "Two Brothers" is being shown at the Jin Cheng Theater, and at the same time, several singers are hired to perform the latest songs and dances of 1936 on stage. The program is exceptionally valuable. Here is a special introduction to these singing and dancing stars:

Ye Ying and Ye Hong are a pair of sister flowers who have just returned from Taiwan. They can both dance and sing, which is truly rare.

Zhang Fan is an innocent child. She is called the Shirley Temple of the Orient.

Yan Fei, she has also just returned from Taiwan. She will soon marry Liu Huan. This is her last performance.

Yan Hua, he is a modern Chinese singer. He will soon go to Nanyang with the Mingming Society to perform, which is naturally considered a farewell souvenir.

Tan Guangyou is a leading figure in the Mingyue Society and a famous villainous young man. "Under the Sword's Edge" and other works are his masterpieces.

Starting today (Friday), the Cathay Grand Theatre will screen Paramount's latest chivalrous and passionate blockbuster, "Rose of the Rancho," starring Glenda Swarthout and John Boles. This time, she dedicates herself to the screen, and although it is her first attempt, she has achieved amazing results. The film's content is also very substantial, and it also features moving songs and unique dances.

Silver Jottings 218

— Zhi Er

The "Song of Everlasting Regret" encountered a lawsuit involving a "Little Lin Daiyu," and Carlo made a few days of business. The second round of screenings by the Central and Southeast theaters also dramatically shut their doors. Commentators say that in the future, when writing screenplays, one should first anticipate the potential for litigation; this is also one of the new advertising techniques of 1936.

When China's second sound detective film, "The Diamond," is released, the advertisement could also use wording such as "Due to the main character issue in this film, the entire publicity department of our company resigned en masse." Compared to "Hundreds of gunshots," perhaps it could sell a few more full houses and produce "China's Third Sound Detective Film."

Bai Yushuang's cameo as Pan Jinlian at the Tianchan Theatre was naturally quite a gimmick. Recently, the Empire Theatre has also been rehearsing an authentic "bouncing opera" version of Pan Jinlian, which is selling out due to Cao Juren's criticism and statement.

Bai Yushuang once wanted to appear on the silver screen, starring in "Begonia Red," but for some reason, it disappeared without a trace. Renewal Issue of "Art Sound" Published 219

The "Art Sound" film and music monthly, edited by Chen Jiazhen, has been popular since its publication. Due to its lively and fresh content, it has been well-received by readers. After active reorganization and improvement, it appears in the publishing industry of 1936 with the greatest effort. The renewal issue was published on March 1st, with even more beautiful content, richer quality, and more lively compilation. The printing of the cover of this issue is extremely magnificent and quite beautiful. The main items of this issue are listed below: Wang Renmei (cover), Anna Sten (back cover), The Success of Movies, Li Keng's Twenty-Four Hours, Illustrated Explanation of Artists (Chen Yanyan), Metal, Wood, Water, Fire, Earth (Caricatures of Movie Stars), Introduction to Anna May Wong, Artists' News, The Correct Way to Learn the Violin, Spring Flower Theme Song, Building Roads Across Borders, New Knowledge Garden, Physical Education, etc.
